                  <h2 class="article--title">
                   Building for a bright future
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  UEFAís new guide for training centre construction and renovation offers clubs and associations important advice for every step.
                 </div>
                </div>

                  <h2 class="article--title">
                   Play-off draw live on Friday
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  In the draw streamed live at 12:00 CET, Czech Republic, Northern Ireland, Portugal, Russia, Switzerland and Ukraine will be drawn into three April ties.

The association club coefficient or country rankings take into account the results of all clubs from each association and are used to determine the number of entries an association is granted for forthcoming seasons.
